},\\n817:             (&mut Percentage(ref mut one), &Percentage(ref other)) => {\\n818:                 one.0 += other.0;\\n819:             },\\n820:             (&mut Number(ref mut one), Percentage(..) | Number(..) => {},\\n826:                 }\\n827:                 debug_unreachable!(\\\"Forgot to handle unit in try_sum_in_place()\\\")\\n828:             },\\n829:         }\\n830: \\n831:         Ok(())\\n832:     }\\n833: \\n834:     fn try_product_in_place(&mut self, other: &mut Self) -> bool {\\n835:         if let Self::Number(ref mut left) = *self {\\n836:             if let Self::Number(ref right) = *other {\\n837:                 // Both sides are numbers, so we can just modify the left side.\\n838:                 *left *= *right;\\n839:                 true\\n840:             } else {\\n841:                 // The right side is not a number, so the result should be in the units of the right\\n842:                 // side.\\n843:                 if other.map(|v| v * *left).is_ok() {\\n844:                     std::mem::swap(self, other);\\n845:                     true\\n846:                 } else {\\n847:                     false\\n848:        // side unit.\\n853:             self.map(|v| v * *right).is_ok()\\n854:         } else {\\n855:             // Neither side is a number, so a product is not possible.\\n856:             false\\n857:         }\\n858:     }\\n859: \\n860:     fn try_op<O>(&self, other: &Self, op: O) -> Result<Self, ()>\\n861:     where\\n862:         O: Fn(f32, f32) -> f32,\\n863:     {\\n864:         use self::CalcLengthPercentageLeaf::*;\\n865:         if std::mem::discriminant(self) != std::mem::discriminant(other) {\\n866:             return Err(());\\n867:         }\\n868:         Ok(match }\\n880:                 debug_unreachable!(\\\"Forgot to handle unit in try_op()\\\")\\n881:             },\\n882:         })\\n883:     }\\n884: \\n885:     fn map(&mut self, mut op: impl FnMut(f32)     Self::Percentage(value) => {\\n891:                 *value = Percentage(op(value.0));\\n892:             },\\n893:             Self::Number(value) => {\\n894:                 *value = /* This Source Code Form is subject to the terms of the Mozilla Public\n2:  * License, v. 2.0. If a copy of the MPL was not distributed with this\n3:  * file, You can obtain one at https://mozilla.org/MPL/2.0/. */\n4: \n5: //! `<length-percentage>` computed values, and related ones.\n6: //!\n7: //! The over-all design is a tagged pointer, with the lower bits of the pointer\n8: //! being non-zero if it is a non-calc value.\n9: //!\n10: //! It is expected to take 64 bits both in x86 and x86-64. This is implemented\n11: //! as a `union`, with 4 different variants:\n12: //!\n13: //!  * The length and percentage variants have a { tag, f32 } (effectively)\n14: //!    layout. The tag has to overlap with the lower 2 bits of the calc variant.\n15: //!\n16: //!  * The `calc()` variant is a { tag, pointer } in x86 (so same as the\n17: //!    others), or just a { pointer } in x86-64 (so that the two bits of the tag\n18: //!    can be obtained from the lower bits of the pointer).\n19: //!\n20: //!  * There's a `tag` variant just to make clear when only the tag is intended\n21: //!    to be read. Note that the tag needs to be masked always by `TAG_MASK`, to\n22: //!    deal with the pointer variant in x86-64.\n23: //!\n24: //! The assertions in the constructor methods ensure that the tag getter matches\n25: //! our expectations.\n26: \n27: use super::{position::AnchorSide, Context, Length, Percentage, ToComputedValue};\n28: use crate::derives::*;\n29: #[cfg(feature = \"gecko\")]\n30: use crate::gecko_bindings::structs::{AnchorPosOffsetResolutionParams, GeckoFontMetrics};\n31: use crate::logical_geometry::{PhysicalAxis,
